The International Cricket Council (ICC) has taken the initiative towards starting the Test Challenge tournament, paving the way for associate member countries to achieve Test status
 test maichon ke is toornament kaa aayojan prayek chaar varsh par sabase nichle darje kii test team or isisi intercontinental cap ke vijeta ke bich hoga
 The ICC decided to hold a test challenge in the two-day board meeting that ended on Thursday, under which associate members would get an opportunity to play a test match
 baithak main board ne prastaav rakhaa ki 31 disambar, 2017 ko yaa us samay chal rahi kisi test shrunkhlaa ke samaapt hone par isisi test team ranking main 10wein sthaan par rahane vaali team aagaamee isisi intercontinental cap kii vijeta team ke khilaaf gharelu maidan par do tathaa anyatra kahin do test match khelegi
 This proposed Test Challenge will be held in the year 2018
 ab isisi ke is nae nirnay kaa arth yah hua ki isisi kii test ranking main sabase nichle paaydaanon par maujuud bangladesh or zimbabwe main se kisi ek team ko pehle test chalange ke dauraan netherland, ireland yaa sanyukt arab emirate jaise kisi ek desh se test darje ke liye bhidana hoga
 Thereafter two ICC Intercontinental Cups are planned to be held during the next 10 years, with the first tournament from 2015 to 2017 and the second tournament from 2019 to 2021
